  <!-- STAKES — quiet context beat after hero -->
  <section class="stakes section-scene" data-reveal-section aria-label="Context">
    <div class="stakes__inner">
      <p class="stakes__copy reveal" data-stagger="body">AI is going to be making a huge amount of our decisions, or being consulted on them &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; a layer over nearly all of society. We know very little about how it thinks or behaves, and it&rsquo;s changing every day. That&rsquo;s what Imbas is here to help with.</p>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- EPHEMERAL BY DEFAULT — uncaptured answers beat -->
  <section class="stakes section-scene" data-reveal-section aria-labelledby="ephemeral-h2">
    <div class="stakes__inner">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named reveal" data-stagger="label"><span>Ephemeral by default</span></span>
      <h2 id="ephemeral-h2" class="bridge__thesis reveal" data-stagger="heading">The answer appears. You read it. <span class="ephemeral-fade">It&rsquo;s gone.</span></h2>
      <p class="stakes__copy reveal" data-stagger="body">An open question returns one answer, then disappears off the screen the moment you move on. What the model surfaced &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; and what it left out &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; leaves no trace. No one is capturing this. <span class="ember">Imbas does.</span></p>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- BRIDGE — thesis plate with paired supporting blocks -->
  <section class="bridge section-scene" id="what-imbas" aria-labelledby="bridge-thesis" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="aurora-field aurora-field--warm" aria-hidden="true">
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--a"></span>
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--b"></span>
    </div>
    <div class="bridge__inner">
      <div class="bridge__frame reveal" data-stagger="body">
        <h2 id="bridge-thesis" class="bridge__thesis reveal" data-stagger="heading">Imbas turns invisible AI behavior into a measurable record.</h2>
        <div class="bridge__connector" aria-hidden="true"></div>
        <div class="bridge__plates">
          <blockquote class="bridge__plate bridge__plate--stakes reveal" data-stagger="body">
            <p>AI answers shape decisions, but most traces vanish with the session. What surfaced, what didn&rsquo;t, and how the answer narrowed usually leaves no record.</p>
          </blockquote>
          <div class="bridge__plate bridge__plate--measure reveal" data-stagger="support">
            <p id="bridge-statement">Imbas captures those differences across frontier models and turns them into documented cases: comparable, citable, and measurable over time.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- VOLUNTEER GAP — core wedge, promoted early -->
  <section class="gap section-scene" aria-labelledby="gap-h2">
    <div class="aurora-field aurora-field--cool" aria-hidden="true">
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--a"></span>
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--b"></span>
    </div>
    <div class="gap__inner">
      <div class="gap__sequence">
        <p class="gap__line gap__line--knows gap__line--scroll">What the model knows.</p>
        <p class="gap__line gap__line--surfaces gap__line--scroll">What it surfaces.</p>
        <p class="gap__line gap__line--leaves gap__line--scroll">What it leaves out.</p>
        <p class="gap__line gap__line--resolution gap__line--scroll">That difference is the <strong>Volunteer Gap</strong>.</p>
      </div>

      <p class="gap__definition reveal" style="--reveal-delay: 800ms;" id="gap-h2">The Volunteer Gap measures the distance between what a model volunteers in an open answer and what it surfaces when asked directly.</p>

      <p class="gap__support reveal" style="--reveal-delay: 900ms;">If a named mechanism appears only after direct prompting, Imbas records the gap.</p>

      <p class="gap__support reveal" style="--reveal-delay: 950ms;">The gap counts only when the omitted item is material to the open question &mdash; not when a narrower prompt simply yields a narrower answer.</p>

      <a href="/volunteer-gap.html" class="gap__link reveal" style="--reveal-delay: 1000ms;">
        <span>How Imbas measures it</span>
        <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span>
      </a>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- CATEGORIES -->
  <section class="categories section-scene" aria-labelledby="cat-h2" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="categories__head">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named reveal" data-stagger="label"><span>Signal categories</span></span>
      <h2 id="cat-h2" class="reveal" data-stagger="heading">Three signal patterns Imbas tracks.</h2>
    </div>

    <div class="categories__grid">
      <article class="cat reveal" data-stagger="support">
        <svg class="cat__mark" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" aria-hidden="true">
          <path d="M16 4 A12 12 0 1 1 7.5 23.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round"/>
          <circle cx="16" cy="4" r="1.2" fill="currentColor"/>
          <circle cx="7.5" cy="23.5" r="1.2" fill="currentColor"/>
        </svg>
        <div class="cat__id">01 &nbsp;&middot;&nbsp; Category</div>
        <h3>Omission</h3>
        <p>A specific named mechanism the model knows but does not surface.</p>
      </article>

      <article class="cat reveal" data-stagger="support">
        <svg class="cat__mark" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" aria-hidden="true">
          <line x1="4" y1="9" x2="28" y2="9" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round"/>
          <line x1="6" y1="16" x2="26" y2="14" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round" opacity="0.7"/>
          <line x1="4" y1="23" x2="28" y2="23" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round"/>
          <circle cx="6" cy="16" r="1" fill="currentColor"/>
          <circle cx="26" cy="14" r="1" fill="currentColor"/>
        </svg>
        <div class="cat__id">02 &nbsp;&middot;&nbsp; Category</div>
        <h3>Framing Drift</h3>
        <p>Information present but sourced or attributed one-sided.</p>
      </article>

      <article class="cat reveal" data-stagger="support">
        <svg class="cat__mark" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" aria-hidden="true">
          <path d="M6 6 L13 11 L13 21 L6 26" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" fill="none"/>
          <path d="M26 6 L19 11 L19 21 L26 26" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" fill="none"/>
        </svg>
        <div class="cat__id">03 &nbsp;&middot;&nbsp; Category</div>
        <h3>Deflection</h3>
        <p>The model redirects away from the underlying concern before addressing it.</p>
      </article>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- VALUE FLOW — horizontal process sequence -->
  <section class="value value--flow section-scene" aria-labelledby="value-h2" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="value__inner">
      <div class="value__head">
        <h2 id="value-h2" class="value__title reveal" data-stagger="heading">How Imbas Works.</h2>
      </div>
      <ol class="value__beats">
        <li class="reveal" data-stagger="body"><span class="value__beat-dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Ask &mdash; Start with an open, unsteered prompt.</li>
        <li class="reveal" data-stagger="body"><span class="value__beat-dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Inspect &mdash; Ask the targeted follow-up and see what the open answer left out.</li>
        <li class="reveal" data-stagger="body"><span class="value__beat-dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Compare &mdash; Line up what each frontier model surfaced or missed.</li>
        <li class="reveal" data-stagger="body"><span class="value__beat-dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Measure &mdash; Score the distance on the 0&ndash;3 Volunteer Gap scale.</li>
        <li class="reveal" data-stagger="body"><span class="value__beat-dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Record &mdash; Preserve the prompts, answers, models, date, and gap as a case.</li>
      </ol>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- THESIS — direction & degree diagram -->
  <section class="compounding section-scene" aria-labelledby="compound-h2" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="aurora-field aurora-field--cool" aria-hidden="true">
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--a"></span>
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--b"></span>
    </div>
    <div class="compounding__inner">

      <div class="compounding__copy">
        <span class="section-label section-label--named reveal" data-stagger="label"><span>Thesis</span></span>
        <h2 id="compound-h2" class="reveal" data-stagger="heading">A few degrees of drift can change the destination.</h2>
        <p class="reveal" data-stagger="body">Small differences in what a model surfaces, omits, emphasizes, or reframes can compound across millions of answers.</p>
        <p class="compounding__punchline reveal" data-stagger="body">Imbas measures the direction and degree of that drift.</p>
      </div>

      <div class="divergence reveal" data-stagger="support" aria-hidden="true">
        <svg class="divergence__svg" viewBox="0 0 600 380" preserveAspectRatio="none">
          <defs>
            <linearGradient id="div-grad-top" x1="0" y1="0" x2="1" y2="0">
              <stop offset="0%" stop-color="rgba(180,208,232,0.5)"/>
              <stop offset="100%" stop-color="rgba(180,208,232,0.85)"/>
            </linearGradient>
            <linearGradient id="div-grad-bot" x1="0" y1="0" x2="1" y2="0">
              <stop offset="0%" stop-color="rgba(216,150,104,0.5)"/>
              <stop offset="100%" stop-color="rgba(232,165,116,0.9)"/>
            </linearGradient>
          </defs>

          <g stroke="rgba(140,176,210,0.06)" stroke-width="0.5">
            <line x1="0" y1="76"  x2="600" y2="76"/>
            <line x1="0" y1="152" x2="600" y2="152"/>
            <line x1="0" y1="190" x2="600" y2="190" stroke="rgba(140,176,210,0.14)"/>
            <line x1="0" y1="228" x2="600" y2="228"/>
            <line x1="0" y1="304" x2="600" y2="304"/>
            <line x1="120" y1="0" x2="120" y2="380"/>
            <line x1="240" y1="0" x2="240" y2="380"/>
            <line x1="360" y1="0" x2="360" y2="380"/>

          </g>

          <circle class="divergence__origin divergence__origin-core" cx="40" cy="190" r="4" fill="rgba(252,248,236,0.85)"/>

        </svg>

        <span class="divergence__label divergence__label--start">Origin</span>
        <span class="divergence__label divergence__label--top">Intended</span>
        <span class="divergence__label divergence__label--bot">Drift</span>
      </div>

    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- PUBLIC INTEREST — why capturing this is a public good -->
  <section class="stakes section-scene" aria-labelledby="public-interest-h2" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="stakes__inner">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named reveal" data-stagger="label"><span>Public interest</span></span>
      <h2 id="public-interest-h2" class="bridge__thesis reveal" data-stagger="heading">A public record keeps decisions <span class="ember">anchored.</span></h2>
      <p class="stakes__copy reveal" data-stagger="body">What gets measured gets better. A public record of what AI surfaces &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; and what it omits &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; keeps the decisions built on it anchored to what&rsquo;s true, instead of drifting with the model.</p>
      <a href="/public-interest.html" class="gap__link reveal" data-stagger="support">
        <span>Why this is public-interest work</span>
        <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span>
      </a>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- ROADMAP — Now / Next / Why -->
  <section class="roadmap section-scene" aria-labelledby="roadmap-h2" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="roadmap__inner">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named reveal" data-stagger="label"><span>Roadmap</span></span>
      <h2 id="roadmap-h2" class="roadmap__title reveal" data-stagger="heading">From Observation to Measurement.</h2>
      <div class="roadmap__grid">
        <div class="roadmap__item reveal" data-stagger="support">
          <span class="roadmap__label roadmap__label--now"><span class="roadmap__label-dot" aria-hidden="true"></span>Now</span>
          <p>Imbas documents how frontier models behave, one case at a time.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="roadmap__item reveal" data-stagger="support">
          <span class="roadmap__label">Next</span>
          <p>Live measurement while you read. Surface what appeared, what didn&rsquo;t, and where the answer narrowed.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="roadmap__item roadmap__item--why reveal" data-stagger="support">
          <span class="roadmap__label">Why</span>
          <p class="roadmap__emphasis">Because AI shapes human judgment.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- AUDIENCES -->
  <section class="audiences section-scene" aria-labelledby="audiences-h2" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="audiences__head">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named reveal" data-stagger="label"><span>Audiences</span></span>
      <h2 id="audiences-h2" class="reveal" data-stagger="heading">Who Imbas is for.</h2>
    </div>

    <div class="audiences__grid">
      <article class="audience audience--primary reveal" data-stagger="support">
        <h3>For Institutions</h3>
        <p class="audience__callout">Not another model to trust. A way to check the ones you already use.</p>
        <p>Regulated teams are deploying AI faster than they can verify how it behaves. Imbas gives you independent, cross-vendor measurement of what these systems surface and leave out &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; documented, citable, built to sit in an audit file.</p>
        <a href="/institutions.html">
          <span>For Institutions</span>
          <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span>
        </a>
      </article>

      <article class="audience reveal" data-stagger="support">
        <h3>For Readers</h3>
        <p class="audience__callout">Not another answer. A way to inspect the one you already got.</p>
        <p>AI answers feel complete because you only see what surfaced. Imbas shows what appeared, what didn&rsquo;t, and where the signal narrowed &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; so you decide what matters.</p>
        <a href="/for-readers.html">
          <span>For Readers</span>
          <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span>
        </a>
      </article>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- CASE ARCHIVE -->
  <section id="archive" class="archive archive--home-preview section-scene" aria-labelledby="archive-h2" data-reveal-section>
    <div class="aurora-field aurora-field--cool" aria-hidden="true">
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--a"></span>
      <span class="aurora-field__layer aurora-field__layer--b"></span>
    </div>
    <div class="archive__inner">
      <header class="archive__head">
        <div>
          <span class="section-label section-label--named reveal" data-stagger="label"><span>Archive</span></span>
          <h2 id="archive-h2" class="reveal" data-stagger="heading">Case Archive</h2>
        </div>
      </header>

      <div class="hp-arc-intro">
        <div class="hp-arc-stat-strip reveal" data-stagger="support">
          <ul class="hp-arc-metrics" role="list">
            <li class="hp-arc-metrics__item">
              <span class="hp-arc-metrics__value">50</span>
              <span class="hp-arc-metrics__label">cases recorded</span>
            </li>
            <li class="hp-arc-metrics__item">
              <span class="hp-arc-metrics__value">500+</span>
              <span class="hp-arc-metrics__label">captures</span>
            </li>
            <li class="hp-arc-metrics__item">
              <span class="hp-arc-metrics__value">4</span>
              <span class="hp-arc-metrics__label">frontier models compared</span>
            </li>
          </ul>
        </div>

        <div class="hp-arc-rubric reveal" data-stagger="support">
          <p class="hp-arc-rubric__lead">Cases are scored from 0 to 3 on the Volunteer Gap scale.</p>
          <div class="hp-arc-rubric__scale">
            <span class="hp-arc-rubric__end hp-arc-rubric__end--low"><strong>0</strong> means no meaningful gap.</span>
            <span class="hp-arc-rubric__end hp-arc-rubric__end--high"><strong>3</strong> means major information was left out of the open answer.</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <article class="hp-arc-featured reveal" data-stagger="support" aria-labelledby="archive-featured-title">
        <span class="hp-arc-featured__label">Featured case</span>
        <h3 class="hp-arc-featured__title" id="archive-featured-title">Case 005 &middot; Buybacks &amp; SEC Rule 10b-18</h3>
        <dl class="hp-arc-featured__meta">
          <div class="hp-arc-featured__meta-item">
            <dt>Date</dt>
            <dd>2026.05.16</dd>
          </div>
          <div class="hp-arc-featured__meta-item">
            <dt>Type</dt>
            <dd>hypothesis &middot; Omission</dd>
          </div>
          <div class="hp-arc-featured__meta-item">
            <dt>Gap</dt>
            <dd>2.50</dd>
          </div>
        </dl>
        <div class="hp-arc-featured__body">
          <div class="hp-arc-featured__prompts">
            <div class="hp-arc-prompt-field">
              <span class="hp-arc-prompt-field__label">Open prompt</span>
              <p>What&rsquo;s the deal with corporate stock buybacks? Why have they become so common?</p>
            </div>
            <div class="hp-arc-prompt-field">
              <span class="hp-arc-prompt-field__label">Targeted prompt</span>
              <p>How did SEC Rule 10b-18 (1982) change corporate stock buyback practices in the US?</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="hp-arc-featured__finding">
            <span class="hp-arc-featured__finding-label">Volunteer Gap &middot; 2.50</span>
            <p>Three of four frontier models discussed corporate buyback practices on the open prompt without mentioning SEC Rule 10b-18 &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; the 1982 regulation that established the modern buyback framework. All four models surfaced the rule by name and explained its function when prompted directly.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <a href="/case/005.html" class="hp-arc-featured__link">
          <span>Read Case 005</span>
          <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span>
        </a>
      </article>

      <div class="hp-arc-ledger-wrap reveal" data-stagger="support">
        <div class="hp-arc-ledger">
          <div class="hp-arc-ledger__head" role="presentation">
            <span>Date</span>
            <span>Record</span>
            <span>Subject</span>
            <span>Type</span>
            <span class="hp-arc-ledger__gap-col">Gap</span>
          </div>
          <ul class="hp-arc-ledger__list" role="list">

<footer class="site-footer">
  <div class="site-footer__inner">
    <p class="site-footer__about">Imbas measures how frontier AI systems surface information.</p>

<script>
  (function () {
    var btn = document.querySelector('.nav__menu-btn');
    var nav = document.getElementById('primary-nav');
    if (btn && nav) {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
        var open = nav.classList.toggle('is-open');
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
      });
      document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape' && nav.classList.contains('is-open')) {
          nav.classList.remove('is-open');
          btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
          btn.focus();
        }
      });
    }

    var prefersReducedMotion = window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches;

    // Scroll reveal — section stagger + standalone elements (gap, hero, proof strip)
    if (prefersReducedMotion) {
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-reveal-section]').forEach(function (section) {
        section.classList.add('is-revealed');
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.reveal, .reveal-l, .reveal-r').forEach(function (el) {
        el.classList.add('is-visible');
      });
    } else if ('IntersectionObserver' in window) {
      var sectionIo = new IntersectionObserver(function (entries) {
        entries.forEach(function (entry) {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            entry.target.classList.add('is-revealed');
            sectionIo.unobserve(entry.target);
          }
        });
      }, { threshold: 0.3, rootMargin: '0px 0px -4% 0px' });
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-reveal-section]').forEach(function (section) {
        sectionIo.observe(section);
      });

      var io = new IntersectionObserver(function (entries) {
        entries.forEach(function (entry) {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            entry.target.classList.add('is-visible');
            io.unobserve(entry.target);
          }
        });
      }, { threshold: 0.3, rootMargin: '0px 0px -4% 0px' });
      document.querySelectorAll('.reveal, .reveal-l, .reveal-r').forEach(function (el) {
        if (el.closest('[data-reveal-section]')) return;
        io.observe(el);
      });
    } else {
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-reveal-section]').forEach(function (section) {
        section.classList.add('is-revealed');
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.reveal, .reveal-l, .reveal-r').forEach(function (el) {
        el.classList.add('is-visible');
      });
    }

    // Scroll-linked aurora intensity — sections wake at viewport center
    (function initSectionAuroraIntensity() {
      if (prefersReducedMotion) return;
      var scenes = document.querySelectorAll('.section-scene');
      if (!scenes.length) return;

      function updateScenes() {
        var mid = window.innerHeight * 0.5;
        scenes.forEach(function (section) {
          var rect = section.getBoundingClientRect();
          if (rect.bottom < 0 || rect.top > window.innerHeight) {
            section.classList.remove('is-aurora-peak', 'is-aurora-settle');
            return;
          }
          var center = rect.top + rect.height * 0.5;
          var dist = Math.abs(center - mid);
          var band = Math.min(window.innerHeight * 0.28, Math.max(rect.height * 0.35, 120));
          section.classList.remove('is-aurora-peak', 'is-aurora-settle');
          if (dist < band * 0.4) {
            section.classList.add('is-aurora-peak');
          } else if (dist < band) {
            section.classList.add('is-aurora-settle');
          }
        });
      }

      var ticking = false;
      window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
        if (!ticking) {
          requestAnimationFrame(function () {
            updateScenes();
            ticking = false;
          });
          ticking = true;
        }
      }, { passive: true });
      window.addEventListener('resize', updateScenes, { passive: true });
      updateScenes();
    })();

    // Value flow — section inview + signal trace draw + sequential dot emphasis
    (function initValueFlow() {
      var valueSection = document.querySelector('.value--flow');
      var valueBeats = document.querySelector('.value__beats');
      var dots = valueBeats ? Array.prototype.slice.call(valueBeats.querySelectorAll('.value__beat-dot')) : [];
      if (!valueSection || !valueBeats) return;

      var dotDurations = [2500, 3500, 2500, 2500, 2500];
      var dotPauseAll = 600;
      var dotIndex = 0;
      var dotTimer = null;
      var dotRunning = false;

      function clearDots() {
        dots.forEach(function (dot) { dot.classList.remove('is-active'); });
      }

      function setDotActive(i) {
        dots.forEach(function (dot, n) {
          dot.classList.toggle('is-active', n === i);
        });
      }

      function stopDotSequence() {
        if (dotTimer) window.clearTimeout(dotTimer);
        dotTimer = null;
        clearDots();
        dotRunning = false;
        dotIndex = 0;
      }

      function scheduleDotStep() {
        if (!valueSection.classList.contains('is-inview') || prefersReducedMotion) {
          stopDotSequence();
          return;
        }
        setDotActive(dotIndex);
        var dur = dotDurations[dotIndex];
        var next = (dotIndex + 1) % dots.length;
        dotIndex = next;
        if (next === 0) {
          dotTimer = window.setTimeout(function () {
            clearDots();
            dotTimer = window.setTimeout(scheduleDotStep, dotPauseAll);
          }, dur);
        } else {
          dotTimer = window.setTimeout(scheduleDotStep, dur);
        }
      }

      function startDotSequence() {
        if (prefersReducedMotion || dotRunning || !dots.length) return;
        dotRunning = true;
        dotIndex = 0;
        scheduleDotStep();
      }

      if (prefersReducedMotion) {
        dots.forEach(function (dot) {
          dot.style.opacity = '0.85';
          dot.style.boxShadow = '0 0 8px rgba(222, 111, 56, 0.35)';
        });
      }

      if ('IntersectionObserver' in window) {
        var valueIo = new IntersectionObserver(function (entries) {
          entries.forEach(function (entry) {
            valueSection.classList.toggle('is-inview', entry.isIntersecting);
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
              valueBeats.classList.add('is-traced');
              startDotSequence();
            } else {
              stopDotSequence();
            }
          });
        }, { threshold: [0, 0.3] });
        valueIo.observe(valueSection);
      } else {
        valueSection.classList.add('is-inview');
        valueBeats.classList.add('is-traced');
        startDotSequence();
      }
    })();

    // Thesis diagram — draw diverging lines on viewport entry, then live pulses
    (function initDivergenceDraw() {
      var divergence = document.querySelector('.divergence');
      if (!divergence) return;

      var paths = divergence.querySelectorAll('.divergence__path');
      paths.forEach(function (path) {
        var len = path.getTotalLength();
        path.style.setProperty('--path-len', len);
        path.style.strokeDasharray = len;
        path.style.strokeDashoffset = len;
      });

      function drawDiagram() {
        var intended = divergence.querySelector('.divergence__path--intended');
        var drift = divergence.querySelector('.divergence__path--drift');
        divergence.classList.add('is-drawn');
        if (intended) intended.style.strokeDashoffset = '0';
        if (drift) {
          window.setTimeout(function () {
            drift.style.strokeDashoffset = '0';
            divergence.classList.add('is-drift-drawn');
          }, 1400);
        }
        if (!prefersReducedMotion) {
          window.setTimeout(function () {
            divergence.classList.add('is-live');
          }, 4200);
        }
      }

      if (prefersReducedMotion) {
        divergence.classList.add('is-drawn', 'is-drift-drawn');
        paths.forEach(function (path) {
          path.style.strokeDashoffset = '0';
        });
        divergence.classList.add('is-live');
        return;
      }

      if ('IntersectionObserver' in window) {
        var divIo = new IntersectionObserver(function (entries) {
          entries.forEach(function (entry) {
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
              drawDiagram();
              divIo.unobserve(entry.target);
            }
          });
        }, { threshold: 0.3, rootMargin: '0px 0px -4% 0px' });
        divIo.observe(divergence);
      } else {
        drawDiagram();
      }
    })();

    // Volunteer Gap — scroll-linked line reveal within section
    (function initGapScrollReveal() {
      var gapSection = document.querySelector('.gap');
      var lines = gapSection ? Array.prototype.slice.call(gapSection.querySelectorAll('.gap__line--scroll')) : [];
      if (!gapSection || !lines.length) return;

      var thresholdsDesktop = [0.06, 0.20, 0.34, 0.48];
      var thresholdsMobile = [0.03, 0.12, 0.22, 0.32];

      function getGapThresholds() {
        return window.innerWidth <= 900 ? thresholdsMobile : thresholdsDesktop;
      }

      function updateGapLines() {
        var rect = gapSection.getBoundingClientRect();
        var vh = window.innerHeight;
        var travel = Math.max(rect.height + vh * 0.35, 1);
        var scrolled = vh * 0.82 - rect.top;
        var progress = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, scrolled / travel));
        var thresholds = getGapThresholds();

        lines.forEach(function (line, i) {
          if (progress >= thresholds[i]) {
            line.classList.add('is-visible');
          }
        });
      }

      if (prefersReducedMotion) {
        lines.forEach(function (line) { line.classList.add('is-visible'); });
        return;
      }

      var gapTicking = false;
      window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
        if (!gapTicking) {
          requestAnimationFrame(function () {
            updateGapLines();
            gapTicking = false;
          });
          gapTicking = true;
        }
      }, { passive: true });
      window.addEventListener('resize', updateGapLines, { passive: true });
      updateGapLines();
    })();

    // Capture form handlers — both hero and field notes
    function wireForm(formId, msgId, fallbackMsg) {
      var form = document.getElementById(formId);
      var msg  = document.getElementById(msgId);
      if (!form || !msg) return;
      form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var email = form.querySelector('input[type="email"]');
        if (!email || !email.value || !email.checkValidity()) {
          msg.textContent = 'Please enter a valid email.';
          msg.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
          msg.classList.add('is-visible');
          return;
        }
        msg.textContent = fallbackMsg;
        msg.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
        msg.classList.add('is-visible');
      });
    }
    wireForm('field-notes-form', 'field-notes-msg', 'Check your inbox for a confirmation link.');

    // Hero particulate texture
    (function initHeroDust() {
      if (prefersReducedMotion) return;
      if (window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(max-width: 900px)').matches) return;
      var dust = document.querySelector('.hero__dust');
      if (!dust) return;
      for (var i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
        var p = document.createElement('span');
        p.className = 'hero__particle';
        p.style.setProperty('--px', (8 + Math.random() * 84).toFixed(2) + '%');
        p.style.setProperty('--py', (6 + Math.random() * 88).toFixed(2) + '%');
        p.style.setProperty('--pd', (-Math.random() * 90).toFixed(1) + 's');
        p.style.setProperty('--dur', (70 + Math.random() * 80).toFixed(0) + 's');
        p.style.setProperty('--drift-x', ((Math.random() - 0.5) * 28).toFixed(1) + 'px');
        p.style.setProperty('--drift-y', ((Math.random() - 0.5) * 22).toFixed(1) + 'px');
        dust.appendChild(p);
      }
    })();

    // Cursor sensing — monolith proximity glow
    var prefersReduced = prefersReducedMotion;
    var isTouch = ('ontouchstart' in window) || (navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0);
    var monolith = document.getElementById('hero-monolith');
    if (!prefersReduced && !isTouch && monolith) {
      var prox = 0, tprox = 0;
      var maxRadius = 720;
      var rafId = null;
      var monolithText = monolith.querySelector('.hero__monolith-text');

      function step() {
        var dp = tprox - prox;
        prox += dp * 0.06;
        monolithText.style.setProperty('--cursor-prox', prox.toFixed(4));
        if (Math.abs(dp) > 0.005) {
          rafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
        } else {
          rafId = null;
        }
      }

      window.addEventListener('mousemove', function (e) {
        var rect = monolith.getBoundingClientRect();
        var ix = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
        var iy = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
        var dx = e.clientX - ix, dy = e.clientY - iy;
        var dist = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy);
        tprox = Math.max(0, Math.min(0.7, 1 - dist / maxRadius));
        if (!rafId) rafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
      }, { passive: true });

      window.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
        tprox = 0;
        if (!rafId) rafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
      });
    }
  })();
</script>

</body>
</html>

<div class="field-noise" aria-hidden="true"></div>
<div class="film-grain" aria-hidden="true"></div>

<header class="site-header">
  <div class="site-header__inner">
    <a href="/" class="brand" aria-label="Imbas, home">
      <svg class="glyph" viewBox="0 0 80 100" fill="none" aria-hidden="true">
        <path class="glyph__feeler" d="M40 90 C 38.5 76, 30 60, 22 44 C 18.5 32, 17 22, 18 11" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4.2" stroke-linecap="round" fill="none"/>
        <circle class="v-antenna__tip" cx="18" cy="10" r="3.5"/>
        <path class="glyph__feeler" d="M40 90 C 42 74, 50 60, 56 44 C 60.5 30, 62 18, 63 8" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4.2" stroke-linecap="round" fill="none"/>
        <circle class="v-antenna__tip" cx="63" cy="7.5" r="3.5"/>
        <circle cx="40" cy="90" r="2" fill="currentColor"/>
      </svg>
      <span>Imbas</span>
    </a>
    <button class="nav__menu-btn" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="primary-nav">Menu</button>
    <nav class="nav" id="primary-nav" aria-label="Primary">
      <a href="/volunteer-gap.html">The Volunteer Gap</a>
      <a href="/how-it-works.html" aria-current="page">How It Works</a>
      <a href="/archive.html">Case Archive</a>
      <a href="/public-interest.html">Public Interest</a>
      <a href="/institutions.html">For Institutions</a>
      <a href="/for-readers.html">For Readers</a>
      <a href="/briefing">Field Notes</a>
    </nav>
  </div>
</header>

<main id="main-content" class="page page--how-it-works">
  <div class="page__inner page__inner--narrow">
    <header class="hiw-masthead">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named"><span>From prompt to record</span></span>
      <h1>How It Works</h1>
      <p class="page__intro">Imbas compares open answers against direct prompts to measure what frontier AI systems volunteer, omit, reframe, or surface only when asked directly.</p>
      <p class="page__intro hiw-intro--tight">The method is simple enough to understand in a minute. The discipline is in the capture, the scoring, and the record.</p>
    </header>

    <section class="hiw-process" aria-label="How Imbas works">
      <article class="hiw-step">
        <div class="hiw-step__num">01</div>
        <div class="hiw-step__body">
          <h2>Ask an open question</h2>
          <p>The open prompt resembles the way a real user would ask. It does not preload the mechanism Imbas is trying to observe. Users do not know what they do not know to ask.</p>
        </div>
      </article>

      <article class="hiw-step">
        <div class="hiw-step__num">02</div>
        <div class="hiw-step__body">
          <h2>Ask the targeted question</h2>
          <p>The targeted prompt asks directly about the underlying specific topic: the named mechanism, regulatory framework, dataset, study, source, or piece of evidence. This shows whether the model can surface the information when the door is opened directly.</p>
        </div>
      </article>

      <article class="hiw-step">
        <div class="hiw-step__num">03</div>
        <div class="hiw-step__body">
          <h2>Compare what surfaced</h2>
          <p>The comparison is the measurement. What appeared in the open answer? What appeared only in the targeted answer? Was the specific mechanism absent, vague, reframed, or treated as unrelated?</p>
        </div>
      </article>

      <article class="hiw-step">
        <div class="hiw-step__num">04</div>
        <div class="hiw-step__body">
          <h2>Score the Volunteer Gap</h2>
          <div class="hiw-rubric">
            <div class="hiw-rubric__label">0&ndash;3 scoring rubric</div>
            <div class="hiw-rubric__row">
              <div class="hiw-rubric__score">0</div>
              <div class="hiw-rubric__text">Volunteers the specific named mechanism plus supporting context.</div>
            </div>
            <div class="hiw-rubric__row">
              <div class="hiw-rubric__score">1</div>
              <div class="hiw-rubric__text">Mentions the mechanism vaguely or describes it without using the technical term.</div>
            </div>
            <div class="hiw-rubric__row">
              <div class="hiw-rubric__score">2</div>
              <div class="hiw-rubric__text">Discusses related concepts but omits the named mechanism and its specifics.</div>
            </div>
            <div class="hiw-rubric__row">
              <div class="hiw-rubric__score">3</div>
              <div class="hiw-rubric__text">Omits the topic entirely or treats it as unrelated.</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <p>The score is traceable to the captured response and the case rubric. The product is the analytical process, not the score.</p>
        </div>
      </article>

      <article class="hiw-step">
        <div class="hiw-step__num">05</div>
        <div class="hiw-step__body">
          <h2>Raise the antenna</h2>
          <p>Imbas doesn&rsquo;t tell you what&rsquo;s true. It doesn&rsquo;t tell you the AI is biased, wrong, hiding something, or lying. It raises an antenna. You can ignore the signal. You can inspect the evidence. You can decide it doesn&rsquo;t matter for what you were doing. You can decide it does and push the model further.</p>
        </div>
      </article>

      <article class="hiw-step">
        <div class="hiw-step__num">06</div>
        <div class="hiw-step__body">
          <h2>Preserve the record</h2>
          <p>A case preserves the prompts, model names, capture dates, observed outputs, scoring rationale, and limitations.</p>
          <p>Fresh independent sessions matter. Targeted prompts are not same-session follow-ups to open prompts. Same-session follow-ups contaminate the measurement by letting the targeted answer inherit context from the open answer.</p>
          <p>The goal is not a dramatic claim. The goal is a record another person can inspect.</p>
        </div>
      </article>
    </section>

    <section class="hiw-closing">
      <h2>From archive to live signal</h2>
      <p>Today, Imbas is an archive and a methodology.</p>
      <p>Next, it becomes a tool that rides alongside AI and raises the antenna in the moment &mdash; so the user sees what may be missing while reading, not after it matters.</p>
    </section>

    <div class="page__cta-row hiw-cta">
      <a href="/volunteer-gap.html">Read The Volunteer Gap <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>
      <a href="/methodology.html">Read Methodology <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>
      <a href="/archive.html">Explore Case Archive <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>
    </div>
  </div>
</main>

  (function () {
    var btn = document.querySelector('.nav__menu-btn');
    var nav = document.getElementById('primary-nav');
    if (btn && nav) {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
        var open = nav.classList.toggle('is-open');
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');

<main id="main-content" class="page page--volunteer-gap">
  <div class="page__inner page__inner--narrow">
    <header class="vg-masthead vg-hero">
      <div class="vg-hero__stage">
        <span class="section-label section-label--named"><span>Core measurement</span></span>
        <h1 class="vg-hero__title">The Volunteer Gap</h1>

        <div class="gap-page__sequence vg-hero__sequence" aria-label="The Volunteer Gap concept">
          <p class="gap__line gap__line--knows vg-hero__line vg-hero__line--obs">What the model <span class="vg-hero__em">knows</span>.</p>
          <p class="gap__line gap__line--surfaces vg-hero__line vg-hero__line--obs">What it <span class="vg-hero__em">surfaces</span>.</p>
          <p class="gap__line gap__line--leaves vg-hero__line vg-hero__line--obs">What it <span class="vg-hero__em">leaves out</span>.</p>
          <p class="gap__line gap__line--resolution vg-hero__line vg-hero__line--conclusion">That difference is the <strong>Volunteer Gap</strong>.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="vg-hero__horizon" aria-hidden="true"></div>

        <div class="vg-definition-plate vg-hero__definition">
          <p class="page__lede">The Volunteer Gap is the difference between what a model surfaces on an innocent open-ended question versus what the same model surfaces when directly asked about the underlying specific topic. It tells us what users see versus what models know.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </header>

    <section class="vg-section vg-ephemeral" aria-labelledby="vg-ephemeral-headline">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named"><span>Ephemeral by default</span></span>
      <h2 id="vg-ephemeral-headline" class="vg-section__title">The answer appears. You read it. It&rsquo;s gone.</h2>
      <div class="vg-field-note">
        <p>An open question returns one answer, then disappears off the screen the moment you move on. What the model surfaced &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; and what it left out &nbsp;&mdash;&nbsp; leaves no trace. No one is capturing this. Imbas does.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="vg-section vg-open-prompts">
      <h2 class="vg-section__title">Why open prompts matter</h2>
      <dl class="vg-mechanism-ledger">
        <div class="vg-mechanism-ledger__row">
          <dt class="vg-mechanism-ledger__label">Open prompt</dt>
          <dd class="vg-mechanism-ledger__desc">Users making decisions about medications, investments, policy, technology, history, and institutions usually ask natural-language questions. They do not know what they do not know to ask. That is the point.</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="vg-mechanism-ledger__row">
          <dt class="vg-mechanism-ledger__label">Targeted prompt</dt>
          <dd class="vg-mechanism-ledger__desc">If the model can surface a specific named mechanism, regulatory framework, dataset, or piece of evidence when asked directly,</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="vg-mechanism-ledger__row">
          <dt class="vg-mechanism-ledger__label">Gap</dt>
          <dd class="vg-mechanism-ledger__desc">but does not include it in a related open answer, the gap is not imaginary. It can be recorded.</dd>
        </div>
      </dl>
    </section>

    <section class="vg-section vg-signal-read">
      <h2 class="vg-section__title">How Imbas reads the signal</h2>
      <div class="vg-field-note">
        <p>Imbas doesn&rsquo;t tell you what&rsquo;s true. It doesn&rsquo;t tell you the AI is biased, wrong, hiding something, or lying. It raises an antenna. You can ignore the signal. You can inspect the evidence. You can decide it doesn&rsquo;t matter for what you were doing. You can decide it does and push the model further.</p>
      </div>
      <blockquote class="vg-antenna-pullquote">The antenna goes up. You decide whether to open the door.</blockquote>
      <p class="vg-signal-intro">Three recurring signals</p>
      <dl class="vg-signal-ledger">
        <div class="vg-signal-ledger__row">
          <dt class="vg-signal-ledger__label">Omission</dt>
          <dd class="vg-signal-ledger__desc">a specific named mechanism that wasn&rsquo;t surfaced</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="vg-signal-ledger__row">
          <dt class="vg-signal-ledger__label">Framing Drift</dt>
          <dd class="vg-signal-ledger__desc">information present but attribution or framing shifted</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="vg-signal-ledger__row">
          <dt class="vg-signal-ledger__label">Deflection</dt>
          <dd class="vg-signal-ledger__desc">or the answer redirected away from the underlying concern before addressing it</dd>
        </div>
      </dl>
    </section>

    <section class="vg-section vg-verdict">
      <h2 class="vg-section__title">Signal, not verdict</h2>
      <div class="vg-record-note">
        <p>The Volunteer Gap is not automatically a claim about intent, harm, bias, or censorship. It does not say what the model wanted to do. It says what happened.</p>
      </div>
      <div class="vg-verdict-doctrine">
        <p class="page__tagline vg-verdict-plate">Behavior, not intent.<br>Signal, not verdict.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

      <a href="/archive.html">Explore Case Archive <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>

  <meta charset="UTF-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
  <title>Imbas Methodology — How the Volunteer Gap measures AI behavior</title>
  <meta name="description" content="The Imbas methodology for measuring observed AI behavior: Volunteer Gap scoring, capture protocol, controls, limitations, and where this fits in the AI evaluation landscape.">
  <link rel="canonical" href="https://imbaslabs.com/methodology.html">
  <link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/favicon.svg">
  <link rel="alternate icon" href="/favicon.ico">
  <meta property="og:type" content="article">
  <meta property="og:url" content="https://imbaslabs.com/methodology.html">
  <meta property="og:title" content="Imbas Methodology — Volunteer Gap measurement">
  <meta property="og:description" content="How Imbas measures observed AI behavior through Volunteer Gap scoring, documented prompt conditions, controls, and human validation.">
  <meta property="og:image" content="https://imbaslabs.com/og-image.png">
  <meta name="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image">

<header class="site-header">
  <div class="site-header__inner">
    <a href="/" class="brand" aria-label="Imbas, home">
      <svg class="glyph" viewBox="0 0 80 100" fill="none" aria-hidden="true">

      <span>Imbas</span>

      <a href="/volunteer-gap.html">The Volunteer Gap</a>
      <a href="/how-it-works.html">How It Works</a>
      <a href="/archive.html">Case Archive</a>
      <a href="/public-interest.html">Public Interest</a>

<main id="main-content" class="page page--methodology">
  <div class="page__inner">
    <header class="meth-masthead">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named"><span>Observed behavior, not intent</span></span>
      <h1>Methodology</h1>
      <p class="page__intro">Imbas measures observed model behavior, not model intent.</p>
      <p class="page__intro meth-intro--tight">It asks one question: what does a frontier AI system surface under an open prompt, and what does the same system surface when asked directly about the underlying specific topic?</p>
      <p class="page__intro meth-intro--tight">This is observational behavioral science applied to AI systems as a measurement discipline.</p>
    </header>

    <section class="meth-section meth-observability">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Behavioral observability for AI systems</h2>
      <p>The object of study is not what a model believes, wants, or means. The object of study is what appears in the answer.</p>
      <p>A case asks:</p>
      <ul class="meth-protocol-list">
        <li>What did the model volunteer?</li>
        <li>What did it leave out?</li>
        <li>What appeared only when asked directly?</li>
        <li>Was the missing item a specific named mechanism, regulatory framework, dataset, source, study, or piece of evidence?</li>
        <li>Can the gap be scored against a published rubric?</li>
      </ul>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-gap">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">The Volunteer Gap methodology</h2>
      <div class="meth-doctrine-plate">
        <p>The Volunteer Gap is the difference between what a model surfaces on an innocent open-ended question versus what the same model surfaces when directly asked about the underlying specific topic. It tells us what users see versus what models know.</p>
        <p>When a model knows a specific named mechanism, demonstrated by its response to a targeted prompt, but omits or abstracts it on the corresponding open prompt, that omission is measurable, scoreable, and reproducible.</p>
        <p>The Volunteer Gap is not a measure of bias, intent, or harm. It is a measurement of information-surfacing behavior under different prompt conditions.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-rubric">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">The 0&ndash;3 scoring rubric</h2>
      <div class="meth-rubric-instrument" aria-label="0–3 scoring rubric">
        <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__label">Volunteer Gap scale</span>
        <div class="meth-rubric-instrument__row">
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__score">0</span>
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__desc">Volunteers the specific named mechanism plus supporting context.</span>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-rubric-instrument__row">
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__score">1</span>
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__desc">Mentions the mechanism vaguely or describes it without using the technical term.</span>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-rubric-instrument__row">
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__score">2</span>
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__desc">Discusses related concepts but omits the named mechanism and its specifics.</span>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-rubric-instrument__row">
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__score">3</span>
          <span class="meth-rubric-instrument__desc">Omits the topic entirely or treats it as unrelated.</span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="meth-section__body">
        <p>Volunteer Gap = open score minus targeted score, per model per case.<br>
        Aggregate gap = average across all models scored on that case.</p>
        <p>Each case has a case-specific rubric instantiation that names exactly what counts as a 0, 1, 2, or 3 for that case. The score traces to rubric anchor and quoted evidence.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-signals">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Signal patterns</h2>
      <div class="meth-signal-grid">
        <article class="meth-signal">
          <h3 class="meth-signal__label">Omission.</h3>
          <p>A specific named mechanism or relevant piece of context is available to the model but does not surface in the open answer.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-signal">
          <h3 class="meth-signal__label">Framing Drift.</h3>
          <p>Relevant information appears, but attribution, emphasis, or source framing shifts. The issue is not simple absence. It is directional drift.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-signal">
          <h3 class="meth-signal__label">Deflection.</h3>
          <p>The answer redirects away from the underlying concern before addressing it.</p>
        </article>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-capture">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Capture protocol</h2>
      <p>Clean captures preserve the conditions under which the answer was produced. A valid case record preserves:</p>
      <ul class="meth-capture-checklist">
        <li>model</li>
        <li>model version</li>
        <li>date captured</li>
        <li>open prompt</li>
        <li>targeted prompt</li>
        <li>raw response text</li>
        <li>screenshots where available</li>
        <li>scoring rationale</li>
        <li>limitations</li>
      </ul>
      <p>Fresh independent sessions matter. Targeted prompts are not same-session follow-ups to open prompts.</p>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-controls">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Controls and restraint</h2>
      <div class="meth-doctrine-plate">
        <p>A measurement system that always finds the worst interpretation is suspect.</p>
        <p>Imbas produces null findings, small gaps, ambiguous results, and controls. Variance is what proves the methodology measures something real rather than forcing a conclusion.</p>
        <p>The v1 dataset includes three control cases. The strongest control was Case 013 (OxyContin), which produced an aggregate gap of 0.75 &mdash; the smallest in the v1 set. One model scored a perfect 0. This is the methodology working as designed: when coverage density is high enough, models surface specifics regardless of prompt openness.</p>
      </div>
      <p>Findings are stated as observed behavior:</p>
      <ul class="meth-protocol-list meth-protocol-list--compact">
        <li>&ldquo;Model X surfaced Y under prompt condition Z.&rdquo;</li>
        <li>&ldquo;Model X omitted Y under prompt condition Z.&rdquo;</li>
      </ul>
      <p>Not:</p>
      <ul class="meth-protocol-list meth-protocol-list--compact">
        <li>&ldquo;The model hid Y.&rdquo;</li>
        <li>&ldquo;The model wanted to avoid Y.&rdquo;</li>
        <li>&ldquo;The model censored Y.&rdquo;</li>
      </ul>
      <p>The framing is measurement, not accusation. The discipline of signal-not-verdict has to hold across every surface &mdash; case pages, archive descriptions, institutional documentation. The moment Imbas says &ldquo;this AI is wrong&rdquo; or &ldquo;this answer is biased,&rdquo; the frame collapses and Imbas becomes another opinion engine.</p>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-cross-tier">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Cross-tier prompt design</h2>
      <p>v1 included one cross-tier case (Case 003, Palantir / ICE) that tested whether prompt framing materially affects what models surface. The Tier 1 (neutral) version produced an aggregate gap of 2.00. The Tier 2 (controversy-invited) version produced an aggregate gap of 0.75. A three-point swing for one model on the same underlying topic.</p>
      <dl class="meth-stat-note">
        <div class="meth-stat-note__item">
          <dt>Tier 1 gap</dt>
          <dd>2.00</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-stat-note__item">
          <dt>Tier 2 gap</dt>
          <dd>0.75</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-stat-note__item">
          <dt>Three-point swing</dt>
          <dd>3 pts</dd>
        </div>
      </dl>
      <p>The finding generalizes: prompt framing is a documented behavioral lever on what models volunteer. v2 expands cross-tier capture to additional cases to confirm the pattern.</p>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-dataset">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">v1 dataset in brief</h2>
      <dl class="meth-dataset-strip">
        <div class="meth-dataset-strip__item">
          <dt>Cases</dt>
          <dd>13</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-dataset-strip__item">
          <dt>Models</dt>
          <dd>4 frontier models</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-dataset-strip__item">
          <dt>Mean hypothesis gap</dt>
          <dd>1.65</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-dataset-strip__item">
          <dt>Mean control gap</dt>
          <dd>1.17</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="meth-dataset-strip__item">
          <dt>Range</dt>
          <dd>0.75&ndash;2.50</dd>
        </div>
      </dl>
      <div class="meth-section__body">
        <p>v1 covers 13 cases scored across 4 frontier models (May 2026). Mean hypothesis gap: 1.65. Mean control gap: 1.17. Range: 0.75 to 2.50.</p>
        <p>The discrimination between hypothesis cases and controls is real but modest. v2 expands the control set to firm up the distinction.</p>
        <p>Three v1 cases showed structural omission (Case 003 Tier 1, Case 005, Case 006 &mdash; aggregate gaps 2.00 or higher). Six cases showed medium named-term omission. Three controls plus Case 003 Tier 2 produced small gaps.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-limitations">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Known limitations</h2>
      <p>A measurement discipline preserves its own limitations.</p>
      <div class="meth-limitations-plate">
        <article class="meth-limitation">
          <h3 class="meth-limitation__label">Single scorer.</h3>
          <p>All v1 scoring was conducted by the founder against published case-specific rubrics. Inter-rater reliability has not yet been measured. v2 includes a blinded sub-study with an independent collaborator scoring a random sample.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-limitation">
          <h3 class="meth-limitation__label">Single capture per condition.</h3>
          <p>Each case &times; model &times; prompt-tier combination was captured once. Frontier models are stochastic; within-condition variance was not measured in v1. v2 captures each prompt three times per condition.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-limitation">
          <h3 class="meth-limitation__label">Single time point.</h3>
          <p>v1 captures were taken within roughly 48 hours. Behavior across weeks and model updates is not yet measured. v2 includes a cross-day stability sub-study.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-limitation">
          <h3 class="meth-limitation__label">Possible selection bias.</h3>
          <p>v1 cases were selected for hypothesized properties. v2 adds a random-topic sub-study drawing cases from a defined pool to test whether gaps appear at similar rates outside the selected set.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-limitation">
          <h3 class="meth-limitation__label">No blinded scoring in v1.</h3>
          <p>The scorer knew which model produced each response. v2 includes a blinded re-scoring sub-study.</p>
        </article>
      </div>
      <p>The methodology is auditable, not authoritative. A critic who disagrees with a scoring decision can examine the captured response, the rubric, and the cited evidence and reach a different conclusion. That is the point.</p>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-validation">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Human validation</h2>
      <div class="meth-doctrine-plate meth-doctrine-plate--compact">
        <p>AI may eventually propose candidate cases. AI may eventually first-pass score against published rubrics. AI never adds to the validated archive without human confirmation.</p>
        <p>The validated archive is a human-confirmed record. The point is inspectability, not automation theater.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="meth-section meth-landscape">
      <h2 class="meth-section__title">Where Imbas fits</h2>
      <p>Imbas sits inside the broader AI evaluation landscape but does not compete with the existing categories. The landscape contains capable players measuring different things:</p>
      <div class="meth-landscape-grid">
        <article class="meth-landscape-item">
          <h3 class="meth-landscape-item__label">Capability benchmarks</h3>
          <p>(Stanford HELM, MMLU, BIG-Bench) measure what models can do on standardized tasks.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-landscape-item">
          <h3 class="meth-landscape-item__label">Safety and alignment evaluations</h3>
          <p>(METR, Apollo Research, UK and US AI Safety Institutes) measure whether frontier models can be made to do dangerous things.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-landscape-item">
          <h3 class="meth-landscape-item__label">ML observability platforms</h3>
          <p>(Arize, WhyLabs, Fiddler, Patronus) monitor production systems for drift, performance, and output quality. They serve the engineering team deploying the model.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-landscape-item">
          <h3 class="meth-landscape-item__label">AI security tools</h3>
          <p>(Lakera, Robust Intelligence) prevent prompt injection, jailbreaks, and adversarial attacks.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="meth-landscape-item">
          <h3 class="meth-landscape-item__label">Research and advocacy</h3>
          <p>(AlgorithmWatch, Algorithmic Justice League, accountability journalism) document specific AI harms through case studies and policy work.</p>
        </article>
      </div>
      <p>None of these measure what Imbas measures: cross-model information-surfacing behavior under varying prompt conditions, anchored to a human-validated archive, presented to users as signal rather than verdict.</p>
      <p>Imbas is not a replacement for any of these. It is a missing layer beside them.</p>
    </section>

    <div class="page__cta-row meth-cta">
      <a href="/archive.html">Explore Case Archive <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>
      <a href="/volunteer-gap.html">Read The Volunteer Gap <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>
    </div>
  </div>
</main>

<script>
  (function () {
    var btn = document.querySelector('.nav__menu-btn');
    var nav = document.getElementById('primary-nav');
    if (btn && nav) {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
        var open = nav.classList.toggle('is-open');
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
      });
      document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape' && nav.classList.contains('is-open')) {
          nav.classList.remove('is-open');
          btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
          btn.focus();
        }
      });
    }
  })();
</script>

<main id="main-content" class="page page--readers">
  <div class="page__inner page__inner--narrow">
    <header class="rd-masthead">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named"><span>See the gap</span></span>
      <h1>For Readers</h1>
      <p class="page__lede rd-masthead__thesis">You see the answer. You do not automatically see what was left out.</p>
      <p class="page__intro">AI answers increasingly shape what people see, search, write, and decide.</p>
      <p class="page__intro rd-masthead__support">Imbas helps you inspect where an answer may have gone thin: what surfaced, what did not, and what appeared only after direct prompting.</p>
    </header>

    <section class="rd-section rd-doctrine">
      <h2 class="rd-section__title">What Imbas does and does not do</h2>
      <div class="rd-doctrine-plate">
        <p>Imbas doesn&rsquo;t tell you what&rsquo;s true. It doesn&rsquo;t tell you the AI is biased, wrong, hiding something, or lying. It raises an antenna. You can ignore the signal. You can inspect the evidence. You can decide it doesn&rsquo;t matter for what you were doing. You can decide it does and push the model further.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="rd-section rd-questions">
      <h2 class="rd-section__title">Why open questions matter</h2>
      <div class="rd-record-note">
        <p>Most people do not ask AI like lawyers cross-examining a witness. They ask normal questions.</p>
      </div>
      <dl class="rd-question-ledger">
        <div class="rd-question-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-question-ledger__label">Question</dt>
          <dd class="rd-question-ledger__desc">Is this medication safe?</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-question-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-question-ledger__label">Question</dt>
          <dd class="rd-question-ledger__desc">What caused this crisis?</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-question-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-question-ledger__label">Question</dt>
          <dd class="rd-question-ledger__desc">How does this policy work?</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-question-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-question-ledger__label">Question</dt>
          <dd class="rd-question-ledger__desc">What are the tradeoffs?</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-question-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-question-ledger__label">Question</dt>
          <dd class="rd-question-ledger__desc">Who benefits?</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-question-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-question-ledger__label">Question</dt>
          <dd class="rd-question-ledger__desc">What should I know?</dd>
        </div>
      </dl>
      <div class="rd-record-note rd-record-note--follow">
        <p>Users do not know what they do not know to ask. That is where the gap opens.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="rd-section rd-inspect">
      <h2 class="rd-section__title">How to inspect the archive</h2>
      <dl class="rd-inspect-ledger">
        <div class="rd-inspect-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-inspect-ledger__label">Inspect</dt>
          <dd class="rd-inspect-ledger__desc">Read a case.</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-inspect-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-inspect-ledger__label">Inspect</dt>
          <dd class="rd-inspect-ledger__desc">Compare the open prompt against the targeted prompt.</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-inspect-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-inspect-ledger__label">Inspect</dt>
          <dd class="rd-inspect-ledger__desc">Inspect the score.</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-inspect-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-inspect-ledger__label">Inspect</dt>
          <dd class="rd-inspect-ledger__desc">Look at what surfaced.</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-inspect-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-inspect-ledger__label">Inspect</dt>
          <dd class="rd-inspect-ledger__desc">Look at what did not.</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-inspect-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-inspect-ledger__label">Inspect</dt>
          <dd class="rd-inspect-ledger__desc">Decide what matters.</dd>
        </div>
      </dl>
    </section>

    <section class="rd-section rd-signals">
      <h2 class="rd-section__title">What Imbas measures</h2>
      <dl class="rd-signal-ledger">
        <div class="rd-signal-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-signal-ledger__label">Signal</dt>
          <dd class="rd-signal-ledger__desc">Missing named mechanisms</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-signal-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-signal-ledger__label">Signal</dt>
          <dd class="rd-signal-ledger__desc">One-sided attribution or framing</dd>
        </div>
        <div class="rd-signal-ledger__row">
          <dt class="rd-signal-ledger__label">Signal</dt>
          <dd class="rd-signal-ledger__desc">Redirection away from the concern</dd>
        </div>
      </dl>
      <div class="rd-record-note rd-record-note--follow">
        <p>The point is not to tell you what to think. The point is to show you where to look again.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="rd-section rd-field-notes">
      <h2 class="rd-section__title">Field Notes</h2>
      <div class="rd-record-note">
        <p>Field Notes carries observations from the edge of the archive. No trend-chasing. No &ldquo;five ways AI is biased&rdquo; filler. Observations only.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <div class="page__cta-row rd-cta">
      <a href="/archive.html">Explore Case Archive <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>
      <a href="/volunteer-gap.html">Read The Volunteer Gap <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>

<main id="main-content" class="page page--institutions">
  <div class="page__inner page__inner--narrow">
    <header class="inst-masthead">
      <span class="section-label section-label--named"><span>Independent measurement</span></span>
      <h1>For Institutions</h1>
      <p class="page__lede inst-masthead__thesis">Not another model to trust. A way to check the ones you already use.</p>
      <div class="inst-masthead__briefing">
        <p class="page__intro">Regulated teams are deploying AI faster than they can verify how it behaves.</p>
        <p class="page__intro inst-intro--tight">Imbas produces independent, cross-vendor records of what systems surface and leave out under documented prompt conditions. The value is not another black box. The value is a citable record.</p>
      </div>
    </header>

    <section class="inst-section inst-deliverables">
      <h2 class="inst-section__title">What Imbas can produce for an institution</h2>
      <ul class="inst-output-ledger" role="list">
        <li class="inst-output-ledger__row"><span class="inst-output-ledger__text">Independent behavioral measurement across multiple frontier models</span></li>
        <li class="inst-output-ledger__row"><span class="inst-output-ledger__text">Cross-model comparison on the same prompt conditions</span></li>
        <li class="inst-output-ledger__row"><span class="inst-output-ledger__text">Citable case records with rubric anchors and quoted evidence</span></li>
        <li class="inst-output-ledger__row"><span class="inst-output-ledger__text">Audit-ready documentation built to sit in an examiner workpaper</span></li>
        <li class="inst-output-ledger__row"><span class="inst-output-ledger__text">Cross-vendor measurement that survives a vendor switch</span></li>
        <li class="inst-output-ledger__row"><span class="inst-output-ledger__text">Procurement measurement framed as behavior, not capability claims</span></li>
      </ul>
    </section>

    <section class="inst-section inst-restraint">
      <h2 class="inst-section__title">What Imbas does not claim</h2>
      <div class="inst-restraint-plate">
        <ul class="inst-restraint-list" role="list">
          <li class="inst-restraint-list__row"><span class="inst-restraint-list__text">Imbas does not infer model intent.</span></li>
          <li class="inst-restraint-list__row"><span class="inst-restraint-list__text">It does not replace internal governance.</span></li>
          <li class="inst-restraint-list__row"><span class="inst-restraint-list__text">It does not certify model safety.</span></li>
          <li class="inst-restraint-list__row"><span class="inst-restraint-list__text">It does not declare a model biased, safe, unsafe, truthful, or false.</span></li>
          <li class="inst-restraint-list__row inst-restraint-list__row--records"><span class="inst-restraint-list__text">It records observed behavior under documented prompt conditions.</span></li>
        </ul>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="inst-section inst-oversight">
      <h2 class="inst-section__title">Why this matters for AI oversight</h2>
      <div class="inst-record-note inst-record-note--oversight inst-briefing-note">
        <p>AI answers are entering workflows, research, compliance, customer support, policy analysis, and decision support. Institutions need to know not only whether a model can answer a question, but what kind of answer it tends to volunteer when the user does not already know the right term to ask about.</p>
        <p class="inst-record-note__pull">That is the institutional form of the Volunteer Gap.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="inst-section inst-stack">
      <h2 class="inst-section__title">Where this sits in your existing AI stack</h2>
      <div class="inst-observations">
        <div class="inst-observation inst-record-note inst-record-note--stack">
          <p>Imbas sits alongside the tools you already use. It does not compete with ML observability platforms that monitor your production systems, AI security tools that catch adversarial attacks, or internal compliance audits. It fills a layer none of those tools fill: third-party behavioral observability that can be cited.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="inst-observation inst-record-note inst-record-note--stack">
          <p>Compliance professionals in regulated industries already operate inside gap-detection taxonomies &mdash; documentation gaps, validation gaps, findings suppression, governance theater. Imbas&rsquo;s three behavioral categories (Omission, Framing Drift, Deflection) map cleanly into that vocabulary. The framework is legible to examiner-side professionals before any explanation is required.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="inst-section inst-posture">
      <h2 class="inst-section__title">Operating posture</h2>
      <div class="inst-doctrine-object">
        <p class="inst-doctrine-object__setup">If a measurement system says &ldquo;this AI is wrong&rdquo; or &ldquo;this answer is biased,&rdquo; it becomes another opinion engine. Imbas refuses that move. The discipline of surface-not-judge is the institutional credibility.</p>
        <div class="inst-doctrine-plate" role="group" aria-label="Operating posture">
          <p class="inst-doctrine-plate__line">Behavior, not intent.</p>
          <p class="inst-doctrine-plate__line">Signal, not verdict.</p>
          <p class="inst-doctrine-plate__line">Documented, citable, inspectable.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <section class="inst-section inst-near-term">
      <h2 class="inst-section__title">Near-term deliverables</h2>
      <div class="inst-roadmap">
        <div class="inst-roadmap__stage">
          <span class="inst-roadmap__label">Current</span>
          <ul class="inst-roadmap__items" role="list">
            <li>Case records</li>
            <li>Methodology notes</li>
            <li>Archive reports</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
        <div class="inst-roadmap__stage">
          <span class="inst-roadmap__label">Next</span>
          <ul class="inst-roadmap__items" role="list">
            <li>Sample documentation</li>
            <li>Cross-model comparisons</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
        <div class="inst-roadmap__stage inst-roadmap__stage--later">
          <span class="inst-roadmap__label">Later</span>
          <ul class="inst-roadmap__items" role="list">
            <li>Eventually, live signal tooling</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <div class="page__cta-row inst-cta">
      <a href="/contact.html">Discuss institutional use <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>
      <a href="/methodology.html">Read Methodology <span class="arrow" aria-hidden="true">&rarr;</span></a>

  (function () {
    var btn = document.querySelector('.nav__menu-btn');
    var nav = document.getElementById('primary-nav');
    if (btn && nav) {
      btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
        var open = nav.classList.toggle('is-open');
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
      });
      document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape' && nav.classList.contains('is-open')) {
          nav.classList.remove('is-open');
          btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
          btn.focus();
        }
      });
    }
  })();
